URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS321402337	2019-01-31 15:58:23	16179	species	Willow Flycatcher	Empidonax traillii			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Clark	US-NV-003		33	USFWS_591		Desert NWR--Corn Creek (Field Station)	L168656	H	36.4387970	-115.3595660	2015-05-19	05:52:00	obsr7422	S23543238	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	142	0.805		3	1	G1280396	0	1	0		This list records the birds encountered by Bob Barnes (Ridgecrest, Kern County, California), Paul Fox (Pacific Palisades, Los Angeles County, California), and Gerry Hawkins (Arlington, Virginia) during a relatively brief early morning visit to Desert National Wildlife Refuge-Corn Creek (Field Station) primarily to look for vagrants at the start of a 3/4 day transect from the desert well up into the Spring Mountains via Lee Canyon to the ski area, the NV Hwy 158 canyon Lee Canyon and Kyle Canyon connector road, and Kyle Canyon including walks at at the junction of Lee Canyon road and the road to Macks group campground, lower and upper Lee Meadows, lower and upper Bristlecone Trail, the paved trail across from Deer Creek picnic area, and Fletcher Canyon Trail. Highlights at Corn Creek included a lengthy experience with an incredibly well seen and heard male Rose-breasted Grosbeak (first called out by Gerry Hawkins) plus a seen and heard singing Bell's Vireo (first called out by Bob Barnes) and at least 50 Western Tanagers.  New Nevada birds for this final day: Sharp-shinned Hawk (Gerry Hawkins only), Sora (Paul Fox only), definitive Anna's Hummingbird, Rose-breasted Grosbeak, and Hooded Oriole (Bob Barnes only). This Corn Creek stop was the start of the 8th and final full day of birding for this southern Nevada birding trip to Clark County Las Vegas area and Lincoln County, Nevada birding sites.
